					.sayHello(request);




		## Streaming n√¢ng cao 
			Server Streaming : X·ª≠ l√Ω c√°c ph·∫£n h·ªìi d∆∞·ªõi d·∫°ng lu·ªìng, ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi vi·ªác truy·ªÅn d·ªØ li·ªáu l·ªõn 
			
			Client Streaming v√† Bidirectional Streaming : T·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a giao ti·∫øp khi c·∫ßn g·ª≠i/nh·∫≠n li√™n t·ª•c d·ªØ li·ªáu theo lu·ªìng .
			
			
		## B·∫£o m·∫≠t (Security ) 
			TLS : gRPC h·ªó tr·ª£ t√≠ch h·ª£p b·∫£o m·∫≠t b·∫±ng TLS, ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o d·ªØ li·ªáu truy·ªÅn ƒëi ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√£ h√≥a 
			
			Authentication : C√≥ th·ªÉ k·∫øt h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c c∆° ch·∫ø x√°c th·ª±c nh∆∞ OAuth2 ƒë·ªÉ b·∫£o v·ªá c√°c d·ªãch v·ª• 
			
			
		## Load Balancing v√† Service Discovery 
			gRPC c√≥ th·ªÉ l√†m vi·ªác c√πng v·ªõi c√°c h·ªá th·ªëng load balancing, service registry ƒë·ªÉ h·ªó tr·ª£ m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng microservices quy m√¥ l·ªõn. 
			
			
			
# ∆Øu v√† nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm c·ªßa gRPC 
	## ∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm 
	
		Hi·ªáu nƒÉng cao: Nh·ªù s·ª≠ d·ª•ng HTTP/2 v√† d·ªØ li·ªáu nh·ªã ph√¢n c·ªßa Protocol Buffers.
		
		ƒêa ng√¥n ng·ªØ: H·ªó tr·ª£ giao ti·∫øp gi·ªØa c√°c d·ªãch v·ª• vi·∫øt b·∫±ng nhi·ªÅu ng√¥n ng·ªØ kh√°c nhau.
		
		T√≠ch h·ª£p streaming: H·ªó tr·ª£ giao ti·∫øp theo lu·ªìng, th√≠ch h·ª£p cho c√°c ·ª©ng d·ª•ng th·ªùi gian th·ª±c.
		
		B·∫£o m·∫≠t v√† qu·∫£n l√Ω l·ªói: H·ªó tr·ª£ deadlines, interceptors, v√† TLS.
	
	
	## Nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm 

			
			ƒê·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p ban ƒë·∫ßu: C·∫•u h√¨nh v√† tri·ªÉn khai ban ƒë·∫ßu ph·ª©c t·∫°p h∆°n so v·ªõi REST.
			
			Kh√¥ng th√¢n thi·ªán v·ªõi tr√¨nh duy·ªát: gRPC truy·ªÅn th·ªëng kh√¥ng l√†m vi·ªác tr·ª±c ti·∫øp tr√™n tr√¨nh duy·ªát (tr·ª´ khi d√πng gRPC-Web).
			
			Y√™u c·∫ßu h·ªçc Protocol Buffers: C·∫ßn l√†m quen v·ªõi ng√¥n ng·ªØ ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a d·ªØ li·ªáu m·ªõi.



# ·ª®ng d·ª•ng c·ªßa gRPC trong th·ª±c t·∫ø 
		Microservices: gRPC l√† l·ª±a ch·ªçn l√Ω t∆∞·ªüng cho giao ti·∫øp gi·ªØa c√°c d·ªãch v·ª• trong ki·∫øn tr√∫c microservices nh·ªù hi·ªáu nƒÉng v√† kh·∫£ nƒÉng m·ªü r·ªông.
		
		H·ªá th·ªëng ph√¢n t√°n: C√°c h·ªá th·ªëng c·∫ßn giao ti·∫øp nhanh v√† ƒë√°ng tin c·∫≠y, ch·∫≥ng h·∫°n nh∆∞ h·ªá th·ªëng AI, machine learning pipeline. 
		
		·ª®ng d·ª•ng th·ªùi gian th·ª±c: C√°c ·ª©ng d·ª•ng c·∫ßn truy·ªÅn d·ªØ li·ªáu streaming (video, chat, telemetry) s·ª≠ d·ª•ng gRPC ƒë·ªÉ gi·∫£m ƒë·ªô tr·ªÖ v√† tƒÉng bƒÉng th√¥ng.


		gRPC l√† m·ªôt framework m·∫°nh m·∫Ω v√† linh ho·∫°t: Kh√¥ng ch·ªâ h·ªó tr·ª£ giao ti·∫øp RPC truy·ªÅn th·ªëng m√† c√≤n t√≠ch h·ª£p c√°c t√≠nh nƒÉng n√¢ng cao nh∆∞ streaming, interceptors, deadlines v√† b·∫£o m·∫≠t.
		·ª®ng d·ª•ng trong th·ªùi ƒë·∫°i ƒëa ng√¥n ng·ªØ v√† microservices: gRPC th·ª±c s·ª± t·ªèa s√°ng khi c·∫ßn x√¢y d·ª±ng c√°c h·ªá th·ªëng ph√¢n t√°n hi·ªáu nƒÉng cao, b·∫£o m·∫≠t v√† m·ªü r·ªông.
		T∆∞ duy v√† c√°ch tri·ªÉn khai chuy√™n s√¢u: Khi thi Java Gold hay x√¢y d·ª±ng d·ª± √°n th·ª±c t·∫ø, hi·ªÉu r√µ gRPC s·∫Ω gi√∫p b·∫°n ch·ªçn l·ª±a c√¥ng ngh·ªá ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi y√™u c·∫ßu c·ªßa d·ª± √°n v√† t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a giao ti·∫øp gi·ªØa c√°c th√†nh ph·∫ßn.
		
		
		
//==========Lesson 49 == Lession 49 == Lession 49 == Protocol Buffer ==========//
	Protocol Buffer (Protobuf) l√† m·ªôt ng√¥n ng·ªØ ƒë·ªãnh d·∫°ng d·ªØ li·ªáu do Google ph√°t tri·ªÉn, ƒë∆∞·ª£c d√πng ƒë·ªÉ serialize d·ªØ li·ªáu nhanh, nh·∫π v√† hi·ªáu qu·∫£ h∆°n so v·ªõi JSON ho·∫∑c XML . C√∫ ph√°p						Vai tr√≤

		## L∆∞u √Ω :

# Ki·ªÉu d·ªØ li·ªáu trong protobuf

# Enum

		UNKNOWN = 0 ;

	üí° L∆∞u √Ω: 
		Enum ph·∫£i c√≥ gi√° tr·ªã m·∫∑c ƒë·ªãnh l√† 0
		Gi√° tr·ªã trong enum ph·∫£i l√† s·ªë nguy√™n  
		


# Nested Message (Message l·ªìng nhau)
	
	message Address {
		string street = 1;
		string city = 2;
	}

	message Person {
		string name = 1;
		Address address = 2; 	// Message b√™n trong message
	
	}



# Repeated Fields (Danh s√°ch )

		repeated string students = 1 	// danh s√°ch h·ªçc sinh 
	}

	üí° L∆∞u √Ω: 
		Kh√¥ng c√≥ List hay Array, ch·ªâ c√≥ repeated

	üí° L∆∞u √Ω: 
		KeyType ch·ªâ c√≥ th·ªÉ l√† string, int32 , int64 , bool 
		ValueType c√≥ th·ªÉ l√† b·∫•t k·ª≥ ki·ªÉu n√†o 
		
		
		
# Optional Fields (tr∆∞·ªùng kh√¥ng b√°t bu·ªôc )

		üí° L∆∞u √Ω: 
			T·ª´ Protobuf 3.15+ optional cho ph√©p ki·ªÉm tra m·ªôt field c√≥ t·ªìn t·∫°i hay kh√¥ng 


# Oneof (Union Field - Ch·ªâ m·ªôt field t·ªìn t·∫°i t·∫°i m·ªôt th·ªùi ƒëi·ªÉm)

# Bytes (L∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu nh·ªã ph√¢n)

# D·ªãch v·ª• gRPC  (Service )

üéØ K·∫øt Lu·∫≠n

//==========Lesson 50 == Lession 50 == Lession 50 == module-info.java ==========//

# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	l√†  file d√πng ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a module trong Java t·ª´ phi√™n b·∫£n 9 tr·ªü ƒëi 
	
		‚úÖ Ki·ªÉm so√°t quy·ªÅn truy c·∫≠p gi·ªØa c√°c module 
		‚úÖ TƒÉng c∆∞·ªùng ƒë√≥ng g√≥i (encapsulation)
		‚úÖ Gi·∫£m k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõng ·ª©n d·ª•ng b·∫±ng c√°ch ch·ªâ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c module c·∫ßn thi·∫øt 
		‚úÖ C·∫£i thi·ªán hi·ªáu su·∫•t kh·ªüi ƒë·ªông c·ªßa ·ª©ng d·ª•ng l·ªõn 
		
		## V√≠ d·ª•

		}
	
# C·∫•u tr√∫c m·ªôt Module trong Java 
	
	
	M·ªôt module ch·ª©a üìÇsrc/com/example/myapp/Main.java 
	üìÇsrc/module-info.java
	
	## V√≠ d·ª• 
		my-module
		‚îÇ‚îÄ‚îÄ src
		‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ com.example.myapp
		‚îÇ   ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Main.java
		‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ module-info.java

	
	üìå Java s·∫Ω t·∫°o file module-info.class khi bi√™n d·ªãch 
	
	
# T·ª´ kh√≥a trong module-info.java 
	
	module           :  Khai b√°o Module 
	exports          :	Xu·∫•t package cho module kh√°c s·ª≠ d·ª•ng 
	requires         :	Khai b√°o module ph·ª• thu·ªôc 
	opens            :	cho ph√©p ph·∫£n x·∫°, √°nh x·∫° (reflection)
	uses             :	khai b√°o module s·ª≠ d·ª•ng d·ªãch v·ª• 
	providers        :	ƒê·ªãnh nghƒ©a d·ªãch v·ª• ƒë∆∞·ª£c cung c·∫•p 
	
	
# üöÄ 4. exports ‚Äì Xu·∫•t Package 
	
	N·∫øu kh√¥ng d√πng exports, package s·∫Ω kh√¥ng th·ªÉ truy c·∫≠p t·ª´ module kh√°c 
	
	module my.module {
		exports com.example.service;
	}
	
		- Ch·ªâ package com.example.service ƒë∆∞·ª£c truy c·∫≠p t·ª´ module kh√°c 
		- C√°c package kh√°c trong module b·ªã ·∫©n 
		
		
# üöÄ 5. requires ‚Äì Khai B√°o Ph·ª• Thu·ªôc
	
	N·∫øu module c·∫ßn d√πng class t·ª´ module kh√°c, ta d√πng requires 
	
	## V√≠ d·ª• 
		
		module my.app{
			requires my.module; // s·ª≠ d·ª•ng my.module 
		}

		
		L∆∞u √Ω : requires s·∫Ω t·ª± ƒë·ªông import t·∫•t c·∫£ c√°c packages trong module my.module 


# üöÄ 6. opens  - M·ªü package cho Reflection 
	
	exports kh√¥ng cho ph√©p reflection (d√πng trong Hibernate . Spring, Gson )
	ƒê·ªÉ d√πng reflection, ta d√πng opens thay v√¨ exports 
	
	## V√≠ d·ª•  
		module my.module{
			opens com.example.model; 		// cho ph√©p reflection 
		}
		
		d√πng opens ƒë·ªÉ Spring/Hibernate c√≥ th·ªÉ truy c·∫≠p private fields 
		
		
# üöÄ uses v√† provides -  C∆° ch·∫ø Service Provider 
		Java h·ªó tr·ª£ d·ªãch v·ª• (Service Provider Interface - SPI) b·∫±ng uses provides 
		
		
	V√≠ d·ª• : 
		
		##üìå B∆∞·ªõc 1 : Khai b√°o interface d·ªãch v·ª• 
			package com.example.service; 
			public interface PaymentService {
				void processPayment(); 
			}
			
		
		##üìå B∆∞·ªõc 2: t·∫°o Module cung c·∫•p d·ªãch v·ª• : 
			module payment.module {
				exports com.example.service;
				provides com.example.service.PaymentService with com.example.service.impl.PayPalPayment
			}
		

		## üìå B∆∞·ªõc 3 : 
		
			module app.module{
				requires payment.module;
				uses com.example.service.PaymentService;
			}
			
			
			- provides ... with ... -> Cung c·∫•p d·ªãch v·ª• 
			- uses  -> Module s·ª≠ d·ª•ng d·ªãch v·ª• ƒë√≥ 




# üöÄ 8. Bi√™n d·ªãch v√† ch·∫°y ch∆∞∆°ng tr√¨nh c√≥ module 
	
	## Bi√™n d·ªãch 
		javac -d out --module-source-path src $(find src -name "*.java")
	
	## Ch·∫°y ch∆∞∆°ng tr√¨nh 
		java --module-path out -m my.module/com.example.myapp.Main
		
		
# L·ª£i √≠ch 
	‚úî TƒÉng b·∫£o m·∫≠t - Kh√¥ng th·ªÉ truy c·∫≠p package n·ªôi b·ªô 
	‚úî Gi·∫£m k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc ·ª©ng d·ª•ng -  Kh√¥ng c·∫ßn ph·ª• thu·ªôc to√†n b·ªô JDK 
	‚úî C·∫£i thi·ªán hi·ªáu su·∫•t -  Load nhanh v√† t·ªëi ∆∞u h∆°n 
	
	
# K·∫øt lu·∫≠n 
		- Module gi√∫p t·ªï ch·ª©c code t·ªët h∆°n v√† tƒÉng b·∫£o m·∫≠t 
		- Kh√¥ng th·ªÉ truy c·∫≠p package n·∫øu kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c exports ho·∫∑c opens 
		- Module gi√∫p Java c·∫°nh tranh v·ªõi h·ªá th·ªëng module c·ªßa OSGi v√† Jigsaw 
		
		
		
# transitive 

	T·ª´ kh√°c transitive trong module-info.java gi√∫p t·ª± ƒë·ªông truy·ªÅn (re-export)	module ph·ª• thu·ªôc ƒë·∫øn c√°c module kh√°c 
	
	- B√¨nh th∆∞·ªùng : Khi module A ph·ª• thu·ªôc Module B, v√† Module B ph·ª• thu·ªôc Module C th√¨ Module A kh√¥ng th·ªÉ d√πng tr·ª±c ti·∫øp Module C 
	
	- Nh∆∞ng n·∫øu requires transitive ƒë∆∞·ª£c khai b√°o , Module A s·∫Ω c√≥ th·ªÉ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c·∫£ Module C  
	
	
	üìå T√≥m g·ªçn: 
		requires -> Ch·ªâ module n√†y d√πng ƒë∆∞·ª£c 
		requires transitive  -> module kh√°c c≈©ng d√πng ƒë∆∞·ª£c
		
		
		
	##üîπ V√≠ d·ª• S·ª¨ D·ª§NG TH∆Ø VI·ªÜN C∆† B·∫¢N 
		üìå module-info.java c·ªßa Module C (cung c·∫•p t√≠nh nƒÉng): 
	
			module moduleC {
				exports com.example.moduleC; 	// xu·∫•t package 
			}
			
		
		üìåCode Java trong Module C 
			package com.example.moduleC; 
			public class CService{
				public static void printC() {
					System.out.println("Hello from Module C!");
				}
			}
		

	##üîπ V√≠ d·ª• Module B - S·ª¨ d·ª•ng Module C 
	
		üìå module-info.java c·ªßa Module B 
		
		module moduleB {
			requires transitive moduleC;	// Xu·∫•t Module C cho Module kh√°c ! 
			export com.example.moduleB; 
		} 
		
			
		üìå Code Java trong Module B 
		
		package com.example.moduleB;
		import com.example.moduleC.CService; // D√πng class t·ª´ Module C
		public class BService {
			public static void printB() {
				CService.printC();
				System.out.println("Hello from Module B!");
			}
		}


	
	##üîπ Module A - kh√¥ng c·∫ßn requires moduleC v·∫´n d√πng ƒë∆∞·ª£c  
	
		üìå module-info.java c·ªßa Module A:
			module moduleA {
				requires moduleB ; 	//  Kh√¥ng c·∫ßn requires moduleC v·∫´n d√πng ƒë∆∞·ª£c  
			}
		
		
		üìå Code Java trong Module A 
			package com.example.moduleA;
			import com.example.moduleC.CService;  // D√ôNG ƒê∆Ø·ª¢C class t·ª´ Module C!
			public class AService {
				public static void main(String[] args) {
					CService.printC();  // G·ªçi tr·ª±c ti·∫øp t·ª´ Module C
				}
			}
			
			üìå L√Ω do? moduleB ƒë√£ requires transitive moduleC, n√™n moduleA c≈©ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√©p d√πng moduleC m√† kh√¥ng c·∫ßn khai b√°o requires moduleC! üöÄ
			
			

# 3. Khi n√†o n√™n d√πng requires transitive?			

	‚úÖ N√™n d√πng khi												
	Module c·ªßa b·∫°n l√† m·ªôt API chung d√πng cho nhi·ªÅu module kh√°c	
	Module B b·ªçc l·∫°i m·ªôt th∆∞ vi·ªán kh√°c (Wrapper Module)
	Mu·ªën t·ª± ƒë·ªông truy·ªÅn ph·ª• thu·ªôc ƒë·∫øn nhi·ªÅu module	
	
	
	‚ùå Kh√¥ng n√™n d√πng khi
	Khi module ch·ªâ d√πng n·ªôi b·ªô, kh√¥ng c·∫ßn module kh√°c bi·∫øt ƒë·∫øn
	Khi b·∫°n mu·ªën gi·ªØ module t√°ch bi·ªát
	Khi c·∫ßn gi·∫£m b·ªõt s·ª± ph·ª©c t·∫°p c·ªßa module

//==========Lesson 51 == Lession 51 == Lession 51 == Reflection ==========//
# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	
	Reflection l√† c∆° ch·∫ø gi√∫p ch∆∞∆°ng tr√¨nh Java c√≥ th·ªÉ ki·ªÉm tra ho·∫∑c thay ƒë·ªïi c·∫•u tr√∫c c·ªßa ch√≠nh n√≥ trong l√∫c ch·∫°y (runtime)
	
	üí° Hi·ªÉu ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n 
		B√¨nh th∆∞·ªùng, b·∫°n d√πng Person person = new Person() ; ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o object 
		V·ªõi Reflection, b·∫°n c√≥ th·ªÉ t·∫°o object, g·ªçi method, truy c·∫≠p field ngay c·∫£ khi kh√¥ng bi·∫øn tr∆∞·ªõc class n√†o s·∫Ω ƒë∆∞·ª£c d√πng 
		
		
	üõ† ·ª®ng d·ª•ng c·ªßa Reflection  
		‚úÖ Framework nh∆∞ Spring, Hibernate - d√πng ƒë·ªÉ inject dependencies(DI) v√† mapping object 
		‚úÖ Gson, Jackson - Chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªïi Object th√†nh Json 
		‚úÖ JUnit - CH·∫°y test case t·ª± ƒë·ªông m√† kh√¥ng c·∫ßn g·ªçi method th·ªß c√¥ng 
		
		
	üî• H√¨nh dung ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n 
		- Gi·∫£ s·ª≠ b·∫°n c√≥ m·ªôt c√°nh c·ª≠a (class), th√¥ng th∆∞·ªùng b·∫°n c·∫ßn ch√¨a kh√≥a(x√°c ƒë·ªãnh class ƒë·ªÉ m·ªü)
		üëâ Nh∆∞ng v·ªõi Reflection b·∫°n c√≥ th·ªÉ b·∫ª kh√≥a, th√°o b·∫£n l·ªÅ ho·∫∑c xem c·∫•u tr√∫c b√™n trong ngay c·∫£ khi kh√¥ng c√≥ ch√¨a ! 
		
		
# C√°c d√πng Reflection trong Java 

	## üîπ L·∫•y th√¥ng tin l√∫c Runtime 
		D√πng Class ƒë·ªÉ l·∫•y th√¥ng tin v·ªÅ m·ªôt class 
		üìå L·ªánh Class.forName("T√™n class") gi√∫p l·∫•y class t·∫°i runtime! 
		
		
		Class clazz = Class.forName("com.example.Person");
		System.out.println("Class Name: " + clazz.getName());

	
	## üîπ L·∫•y danh s√°ch Constructor 

		Constructor[] constructors = clazz.getDeclaredConstructors();
		for (Constructor constructor : constructors) {
			System.out.println("Constructor: " + constructor);
		}



	## üîπ L·∫•y danh s√°ch Field (bi·∫øn)
	
		Field[] fields = clazz.getDeclaredFields();
		for (Field field : fields) {
			System.out.println("Field: " + field.getName());
		}


	## üîπ L·∫•y danh s√°ch Method 
	
		Method[] methods = clazz.getDeclaredMethods();
		for (Method method : methods) {
			System.out.println("Method: " + method.getName());
		}

		

	## üîπ Truy c·∫≠p Field private (Hack bi·∫øn private)
		B√¨nh th∆∞·ªùng kh√¥ng th·ªÉ truy c·∫≠p bi·∫øn private, nh∆∞ng v·ªõi Reflection th√¨ c√≥ th·ªÉ:
		
		Person person = new Person();
		Field nameField = clazz.getDeclaredField("name");
		nameField.setAccessible(true); // Bypass private!
		nameField.set(person, "John Doe"); // G√°n gi√° tr·ªã m·ªõi
		System.out.println(person.getName()); // In ra John Doe

	üö® L∆∞u √Ω: Vi·ªác n√†y ph√° v·ª° nguy√™n t·∫Øc ƒë√≥ng g√≥i (encapsulation), n√™n ch·ªâ d√πng khi th·ª±c s·ª± c·∫ßn
	
	
	## üîπ G·ªçi Method t·∫°i runtime 
		Method method = clazz.getDeclaredMethod("sayHello");
		method.invoke(person);  // G·ªçi sayHello() m√† kh√¥ng c·∫ßn bi·∫øt tr∆∞·ªõc class
 
		üìå ·ª®ng d·ª•ng: Spring d√πng ƒë·ªÉ g·ªçi Bean method t·ª± ƒë·ªông.

	

	## üîπ T·∫°o Object t·∫°i runtime 
	
		Constructor constructor = clazz.getDeclaredConstructor();
		Person person = (Person) constructor.newInstance(); // T·∫°o object
		System.out.println(person);



# 	Khi n√†o n√™n v√† kh√¥ng n√™n d√πng Reflection? 

‚úÖ N√™n d√πng khi															‚ùå Kh√¥ng n√™n d√πng khi
D√πng trong framework nh∆∞ Spring, Hibernate							Khi hi·ªáu su·∫•t quan tr·ªçng
Test Automation (JUnit, Mockito)									Khi kh√¥ng c·∫ßn thay ƒë·ªïi class l√∫c runtime
X√¢y d·ª±ng Plugin, Dependency Injection								Khi c√≥ th·ªÉ d√πng c√°ch kh√°c t·ªët h∆°n


# H·∫°n ch·∫ø c·ªßa Reflection
‚ùå Hi·ªáu su·∫•t th·∫•p h∆°n do ph·∫£i truy v·∫•n metadata class.
‚ùå B·ªè qua t√≠nh ƒë√≥ng g√≥i (private, protected c√≥ th·ªÉ b·ªã truy c·∫≠p).
‚ùå D·ªÖ l·ªói n·∫øu class b·ªã ƒë·ªïi t√™n (Refactor t√™n class c√≥ th·ªÉ g√¢y l·ªói runtime).


üî• K·∫øt lu·∫≠n
‚úî Reflection gi√∫p ta kh√°m ph√° v√† thao t√°c v·ªõi class t·∫°i runtime.
‚úî R·∫•t m·∫°nh m·∫Ω nh∆∞ng c·∫ßn d√πng c·∫©n th·∫≠n ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh gi·∫£m hi·ªáu su·∫•t.
‚úî H·ªØu √≠ch trong Spring, Hibernate, JUnit, v√† nhi·ªÅu framework kh√°c.


//==========Lesson 52 == Lession 52 == Lession 52 == SingleThreadModel Interface ==========//
	
# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	SingleThreadModel l√† m·ªôt interface c≈© trong Java Servlet API gi√∫p ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o r·∫±ng m·ªói request ƒë·∫øn m·ªôt servlet s·∫Ω ƒë∆∞·ª£c x·ª≠ l√Ω b·ªüi m·ªôt intance ri√™ng bi·ªát c·ªßa servlet ƒë√≥. 
		
		üí° T√≥m g·ªçn: 
			- D√πng trong servlet ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a (thread safety)
			- M·ªói request ƒë∆∞·ª£c x·ª≠ l√Ω b·ªüi m·ªôt instance servlet ri√™ng bi·ªát 
			- ƒê√£ b·ªã deprecated t·ª´ Servlet 2.4 v√† lo·∫°i b·ªè t·ª´ Servlet 2.5 tr·ªü ƒëi 
			
			
# C√°ch ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông  
				
	Khi m·ªôt servlet implement SingleThreadModel, server c√≥ hai c√°ch x·ª≠ l√Ω request:

	T·∫°o m·ªôt instance servlet m·ªõi cho m·ªói request.
	D√πng m·ªôt pool servlet instance ƒë·ªÉ x·ª≠ l√Ω nhi·ªÅu request song song.
	üí° L√Ω do: Servlet b·∫£n ch·∫•t l√† ƒëa lu·ªìng (multi-threaded), n·∫øu nhi·ªÅu request ƒë·∫øn c√πng l√∫c, c√≥ th·ªÉ g√¢y ra v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ race condition n·∫øu servlet c√≥ bi·∫øn instance chung


	## üìå V√≠ d·ª•: Servlet kh√¥ng thread-safe 
		@WebServlet("/unsafe")
		public class UnsafeServlet extends HttpServlet {
			private int counter = 0;  // Bi·∫øn instance d√πng chung
		
			protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
				counter++;  // C√≥ th·ªÉ b·ªã ghi ƒë√® b·ªüi nhi·ªÅu lu·ªìng kh√°c nhau!
				resp.getWriter().println("Counter: " + counter);
			}
		}
		
			‚ö† L·ªói c√≥ th·ªÉ x·∫£y ra: 
			N·∫øu 2 request ch·∫°y song song, bi·∫øn counter c√≥ th·ªÉ b·ªã ghi ƒë√® kh√¥ng mong mu·ªën, d·∫´n ƒë·∫øn bug d·ªØ li·ªáu.
			
			
			
	## 		üìå D√πng SingleThreadModel ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh l·ªói tr√™n 
			@WebServlet("/safe")
			public class SafeServlet extends HttpServlet implements SingleThreadModel {
				private int counter = 0;  // Bi·∫øn instance kh√¥ng b·ªã truy c·∫≠p ƒë·ªìng th·ªùi
			
				protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
					counter++;  
					resp.getWriter().println("Counter: " + counter);
				}
			}

			üöÄ L√∫c n√†y, m·ªói request c√≥ m·ªôt instance servlet ri√™ng, tr√°nh ƒë∆∞·ª£c l·ªói ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
			
			
# 		3. T·∫°i sao SingleThreadModel b·ªã lo·∫°i b·ªè?	

			üö® H·∫°n ch·∫ø l·ªõn c·ªßa SingleThreadModel:
			‚ùå Nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm										‚ö° Gi·∫£i th√≠ch
			T·ªën b·ªô nh·ªõ											V√¨ m·ªói request c√≥ m·ªôt servlet ri√™ng, n√™n server ph·∫£i qu·∫£n l√Ω nhi·ªÅu instance servlet.
			Kh√¥ng th·ª±c s·ª± an to√†n								N·∫øu servlet c√≥ bi·∫øn static ho·∫∑c d√πng shared resource (file, DB), th√¨ v·∫´n b·ªã v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
			Kh√¥ng ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi h·ªá th·ªëng l·ªõn						V·ªõi h·ªá th·ªëng nhi·ªÅu request, vi·ªác t·∫°o nhi·ªÅu instance servlet s·∫Ω l√†m gi·∫£m hi·ªáu su·∫•t.
			
			üí° Thay v√†o ƒë√≥, n√™n d√πng synchronized, ThreadLocal ho·∫∑c Stateless Servlet.
			
			
			
# 4. C√°ch thay th·∫ø SingleThreadModel 
				
			
	## üîπ C√°ch 1: D√πng synchronized (Kh√¥ng khuy·∫øn kh√≠ch) 
		ƒê·∫∑t synchronized v√†o doGet() ho·∫∑c doPost(), nh∆∞ng l√†m gi·∫£m hi·ªáu su·∫•t.
				@WebServlet("/sync")
				public class SyncServlet extends HttpServlet {
					private int counter = 0;
				
					protected synchronized void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
						counter++;
						resp.getWriter().println("Counter: " + counter);
					}
				}

					‚ö† Nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm:
		
					T·∫•t c·∫£ request ph·∫£i ch·ªù nhau, gi·∫£m t·ªëc ƒë·ªô x·ª≠ l√Ω.
			
			
			
			
	## 	üîπ C√°ch 2: D√πng ThreadLocal ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o bi·∫øn ri√™ng cho t·ª´ng request	
	
	
			@WebServlet("/threadlocal")
			public class ThreadLocalServlet extends HttpServlet {
				private ThreadLocal counter = ThreadLocal.withInitial(() -> 0);
			
				protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
					counter.set(counter.get() + 1);
					resp.getWriter().println("Counter: " + counter.get());
				}
			}
	
			üöÄ ∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm:
			Kh√¥ng c·∫ßn ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
			M·ªói request c√≥ m·ªôt bi·∫øn ri√™ng, tr√°nh l·ªói race condition.	üöÄ ∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm:
			
			Kh√¥ng c·∫ßn ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
			M·ªói request c√≥ m·ªôt bi·∫øn ri√™ng, tr√°nh l·ªói race condition.
			
			
			
	## 	üîπ C√°ch 3: D√πng Stateless Servlet (C√°ch t·ªët nh·∫•t)
			
			Kh√¥ng d√πng bi·∫øn instance ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
			üìå V√≠ d·ª•: Servlet Stateless
			
			@WebServlet("/stateless")
			public class StatelessServlet extends HttpServlet {
				protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
					int counter = Integer.parseInt(req.getParameter("count")); // Kh√¥ng d√πng bi·∫øn instance
					resp.getWriter().println("Counter: " + (counter + 1));
				}
			}

			‚úÖ L·ª£i √≠ch:

Servlet kh√¥ng gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i, m·ªçi request ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p v·ªõi nhau.
Kh√¥ng lo l·∫Øng v·ªÅ ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a hay b·ªô nh·ªõ.
			


//==========Lesson 53 == Lession 53 == Lession 53 == ThreadLocal & Stateless Servlet ==========//

# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	Trong thi·∫øt k·∫ø h·ªá th·ªëng hi·ªáu su·∫•t cao, vi·ªác qu·∫£n l√Ω d·ªØ li·ªáu thread-safe m√† v·∫´n ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o hi·ªáu su·∫•t t·ªët l√† m·ªôt b√†i to√°n quan tr·ªçng. ThreadLocal v√† Stateless Servlet l√† hai c√°ch ph·ªï bi·∫øn gi√∫p gi·∫£i quy·∫øt v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ n√†y. 
	
//------------------ ThreadLocal - Qu·∫£n l√Ω bi·∫øn theo t·ª´ng thread 

# üîπ Kh√°i ni·ªám  
		ThreadLocal l√† m·ªôt bi·∫øn c·ª•c b·ªô theo thread, c√≥ nghƒ©a l√† m·ªói thread c√≥ m·ªôt b·∫£n sao ri√™ng bi·ªát c·ªßa bi·∫øn ƒë√≥. N√≥ gi√∫p l∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p cho t·ª´ng thread, tr√°nh t√¨nh tr·∫°ng race condition trong m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng ƒëa lu·ªìng
		
# üîπ ·ª®ng d·ª•ng ch√≠nh c·ªßa ThreadLocal : 
		- L∆∞u th√¥ng tin request, user session, transaction trong ƒëa lu·ªìng 
		- T·∫°o m·ªôt b·ªô nh·ªõ cache c·ª•c b·ªô theo t·ª´ng thread 
		- Qu·∫£n l√Ω context nh∆∞ database connection ho·∫∑c Spring Security Context 
		
# 	üîπ C√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ThreadLocal 

		## üìå D√πng ThreadLocal ƒë·ªÉ l∆∞u bi·∫øn user cho t·ª´ng request

			public class UserContext {
				private static final ThreadLocal currentUser = ThreadLocal.withInitial(() -> "Guest");
			
				public static void setUser(String user) {
					currentUser.set(user);
				}
			
				public static String getUser() {
					return currentUser.get();
				}
			
				public static void clear() {
					currentUser.remove(); // Gi·∫£i ph√≥ng t√†i nguy√™n tr√°nh memory leak
				}
			}


		## üìå C√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ThreadLocal trong servlet 
			@WebServlet("/threadlocal")
			public class ThreadLocalServlet extends HttpServlet {
				protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
					String user = req.getParameter("user");
					UserContext.setUser(user); // L∆∞u user v√†o ThreadLocal
			
					resp.getWriter().println("Current User: " + UserContext.getUser());
			
					UserContext.clear(); // X√≥a sau khi d√πng ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh memory leak
				}
			}
			

# ‚úÖ L·ª£i √≠ch: 
		M·ªói thread c√≥ m·ªôt bi·∫øn (curentUser) ri√™ng, tr√°nh l·ªói race condition . 
		Kh√¥ng c·∫ßn ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a(synchronized), gi√∫p c·∫£i thi·ªán hi·ªáu su·∫•t . 


# ‚ö† L∆∞u √Ω quan tr·ªçng 
		- Nh·ªõ g·ªçi remove() sau khi s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ! N·∫øu kh√¥ng, d·ªØ li·ªáu c·ªßa thread c≈© c√≥ th·ªÉ b·ªã t√°i s·ª≠ d·ª•ng trong thread pool, g√¢y l·ªói b·∫£o m·∫≠t 
		- Kh√¥ng s·ª≠ d·ª•ng trong ·ª©ng d·ª•ng c√≥ nhi·ªÅu t·∫ßng (distributed system), v√¨ ThreadLocal ch·ªâ ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông trong JVM 
		
		

# üîπ ·ª®ng d·ª•ng th·ª±c t·∫ø c·ªßa ThreadLocal 
	
	## Qu·∫£n l√Ω Transactional trong JDBC 
		public class ConnectionManager {
			private static final ThreadLocal connectionHolder = new ThreadLocal<>();
		
			public static void setConnection(Connection conn) {
				connectionHolder.set(conn);
			}
		
			public static Connection getConnection() {
				return connectionHolder.get();
			}
		
			public static void clear() {
				connectionHolder.remove();
			}
		}
		
		üî• Trong h·ªá th·ªëng th·ª±c t·∫ø, Spring ƒë√£ t√≠ch h·ª£p ThreadLocal ƒë·ªÉ qu·∫£n l√Ω transaction trong Hibernate.	



//------------------ @Transactional th·ª±c s·ª± l√†m g√¨ 
	
# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	Khi b·∫°n g·∫Øn @Transactional v√†o m·ªôt method ho·∫∑c class trong Spring:
	‚úÖ Spring b·∫Øt ƒë·∫ßu m·ªôt transaction tr∆∞·ªõc khi method ch·∫°y.
	‚úÖ N·∫øu method ch·∫°y th√†nh c√¥ng, transaction s·∫Ω commit (l∆∞u thay ƒë·ªïi v√†o DB).
	‚úÖ N·∫øu method g·∫∑p l·ªói (throw Exception), transaction s·∫Ω rollback (h·ªßy b·ªè thay ƒë·ªïi).


# V√≠ d·ª• c∆° b·∫£n 
	
		@Service
		public class UserService {
			@Transactional
			public void createUser(User user) {
				userRepository.save(user); // L∆∞u v√†o DB
				sendEmail(user.getEmail()); // N·∫øu l·ªói ·ªü ƒë√¢y, transaction s·∫Ω rollback
			}
		}
			
		‚û° N·∫øu sendEmail() n√©m l·ªói (Exception), userRepository.save(user) c≈©ng b·ªã rollback, t·ª©c l√† d·ªØ li·ªáu s·∫Ω kh√¥ng l∆∞u v√†o DB.



# Nh·ªØng l·ªói ph·ªï bi·∫øn khi d√πng @Transactional

	## ‚ùå 2.1. G·ªçi @Transactional t·ª´ ch√≠nh class c·ªßa n√≥ 
		Spring d√πng proxy ƒë·ªÉ qu·∫£n l√Ω @Transactional. N·∫øu b·∫°n g·ªçi method t·ª´ c√πng m·ªôt class, transaction s·∫Ω kh√¥ng ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông 
		
			### ‚ö† Sai c√°ch

				@Service
				public class UserService {
					@Transactional
					public void createUser(User user) {
						userRepository.save(user);
					}
				
					public void registerUser(User user) {
						createUser(user); // ‚ùå G·ªçi t·ª´ ch√≠nh class -> Transaction kh√¥ng ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông!
					}
				}



			### ‚úÖ ƒê√∫ng c√°ch
				- G·ªçi t·ª´ class kh√°c ho·∫∑c d√πng @Autowired ch√≠nh class c·ªßa n√≥ 
				
						@Service
						public class UserService {
							@Autowired
							private UserService self; // Inject ch√≠nh n√≥
						
							@Transactional
							public void createUser(User user) {
								userRepository.save(user);
							}
						
							public void registerUser(User user) {
								self.createUser(user); // ‚úÖ Transaction ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông
							}
						}



			### üí° C√°ch t·ªët h∆°n: T√°ch th√†nh m·ªôt service kh√°c. 
			
			
						@Service
						public class UserTransactionService {
							@Transactional
							public void createUser(User user) {
								userRepository.save(user);
							}
						}
						
						
						
						@Service
						public class UserService {
							@Autowired
							private UserTransactionService userTransactionService;
						
							public void registerUser(User user) {
								userTransactionService.createUser(user); // ‚úÖ Transaction ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông
							}
						}





	## ‚ùå 2.2. Kh√¥ng ƒë·∫∑t @Transactional ·ªü m·ª©c public 
		Spring ch·ªâ √°p d·ª•ng transactional tr√™n c√°c method public. N·∫øu d√πng private ho·∫∑c protected, transaction kh√¥ng c√≥ hi·ªáu l·ª±c 
			
			
			### ‚ö† Sai c√°ch 
			
			
					@Service
					public class UserService {
						@Transactional
						private void createUser(User user) { // ‚ùå Kh√¥ng ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông v√¨ kh√¥ng ph·∫£i public
							userRepository.save(user);
						}
					}

			### ‚úÖ C√°ch ƒë√∫ng 
			
					@Service
					public class UserService {
						@Transactional
						public void createUser(User user) { // ‚úÖ B·∫Øt bu·ªôc ph·∫£i l√† public
							userRepository.save(user);
						}
					}

				


	## ‚ùå 2.3. Ch·ªâ RuntimeException m·ªõi k√≠ch ho·∫°t rollback 
	
		M·∫∑c ƒë·ªãnh, @Transactional ch·ªâ rollback khi g·∫∑p RuntimeException ho·∫∑c Error. N·∫øu method n√©m Checked Exception , n√≥ s·∫Ω kh√¥ng rollback 
		
		
			### ‚ö† Sai c√°ch
				

					@Service
					public class UserService {
						@Transactional
						public void createUser(User user) throws Exception { 
							userRepository.save(user);
							throw new Exception("Checked Exception x·∫£y ra"); // ‚ùå Kh√¥ng rollback!
						}
					}

			### ‚úÖ C√°ch ƒë√∫ng 
				C·∫•u h√¨nh @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class):
				
					@Service
					public class UserService {
						@Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
						public void createUser(User user) throws Exception {
							userRepository.save(user);
							throw new Exception("Checked Exception x·∫£y ra"); // ‚úÖ Rollback ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông
						}
					}
					


	## ‚ùå 2.4. Kh√¥ng ƒë·∫∑t @Transactional ƒë√∫ng ch·ªó
		
		### ‚ö† Sai: ƒê·∫∑t tr√™n Controller 
			
				@RestController
				@RequestMapping("/users")
				public class UserController {
					@Transactional // ‚ùå Sai! Kh√¥ng n√™n ƒë·∫∑t ·ªü Controller
					@PostMapping
					public void createUser(@RequestBody User user) {
						userService.createUser(user);
					}
				}

		
		### ‚úÖ ƒê√∫ng: ƒê·∫∑t tr√™n Service
		
				@Service
				public class UserService {
					@Transactional // ‚úÖ ƒê·∫∑t ·ªü Service
					public void createUser(User user) {
						userRepository.save(user);
					}
				}



# C√°c m·ª©c c√°ch ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông c·ªßa Transactional 
		
		
		M·ª©c ƒë·ªô Isolation					M√¥ t·∫£
		DEFAULT						D√πng m·ª©c c·ªßa DB (th∆∞·ªùng l√† READ COMMITTED).
		READ UNCOMMITTED			Th·∫•p nh·∫•t, ƒë·ªçc d·ªØ li·ªáu ch∆∞a commit (d·ªÖ b·ªã l·ªói Dirty Read).
		READ COMMITTED				Ch·ªâ ƒë·ªçc d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë√£ commit (tr√°nh Dirty Read).
		REPEATABLE READ				ƒê·ªçc d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªëng nhau trong c√πng m·ªôt transaction (tr√°nh Phantom Read).
		SERIALIZABLE				Cao nh·∫•t, ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o kh√¥ng c√≥ xung ƒë·ªôt d·ªØ li·ªáu.




		### üìå V√≠ d·ª•: C·∫•u h√¨nh Isolation Level 
		
		
			@Transactional(isolation = Isolation.REPEATABLE_READ)
			public void updateUserBalance(Long userId, BigDecimal amount) {
				User user = userRepository.findById(userId).orElseThrow();
				user.setBalance(user.getBalance().add(amount));
				userRepository.save(user);
			}


# K·∫øt lu·∫≠n : D√πng @Transactional th·∫ø n√†o cho ƒë√∫ng ? 
	
		‚úÖ Lu√¥n ƒë·∫∑t @Transactional ·ªü Service, kh√¥ng ƒë·∫∑t ·ªü Controller.
		‚úÖ Kh√¥ng g·ªçi method @Transactional t·ª´ ch√≠nh class c·ªßa n√≥.
		‚úÖ Ch·ªâ rollback v·ªõi RuntimeException, n·∫øu mu·ªën rollback Exception th√¨ ph·∫£i d√πng rollbackFor = Exception.class.
		‚úÖ Nh·ªõ ƒë·∫∑t method l√† public, v√¨ Spring ch·ªâ qu·∫£n l√Ω giao d·ªãch tr√™n method public.
		‚úÖ C·∫©n th·∫≠n v·ªõi thread pool, async ho·∫∑c c√°c method ch·∫°y song song, v√¨ @Transactional ch·ªâ ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông trong c√πng m·ªôt thread.





//----------------------- Stateless Servlet -  Ki·∫øn tr√∫c kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i 

# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	üîπ Stateless Servlet l√† g√¨? 
		Trong thi·∫øt k·∫ø web hi·ªán ƒë·∫°i, Stateless Servlet l√† m·ªôt servlet kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i tr√™n instance, nghƒ©a l√†: 
			- Kh√¥ng l∆∞u bi·∫øn instance(private int counter;) ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh l·ªói ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
			- D·ªØ li·ªáu request ƒë·∫øn v√† ƒëi m·ªôt c√°ch ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p, kh√¥ng ph·ª• thu·ªôc v√†o tr·∫°ng th√°i c≈©. 
			
	üí° ·ª®ng d·ª•ng ch√≠nh c·ªßa Stateless Servlet 
		X√¢y d·ª±ng RESTful API.
		Thi·∫øt k·∫ø h·ªá th·ªëng m·ªü r·ªông d·ªÖ d√†ng (scalable)
		T√≠ch h·ª£p v·ªõi microservices ƒë·ªÉ gi·∫£m ph·ª• thu·ªôc 

	
# C√°ch tri·ªÉn khai State Servlet 
	
	###üìå V√≠ d·ª• 1: Stateless Servlet ch·ªâ x·ª≠ l√Ω request m√† kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i  
	
			@WebServlet("/stateless")
			public class StatelessServlet extends HttpServlet {
				protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
					String user = req.getParameter("user");
					resp.getWriter().println("Hello, " + user);
				}
			}


		üî• ∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm c·ªßa Stateless Servlet:
		‚úî Kh√¥ng l∆∞u bi·∫øn instance ‚Üí Kh√¥ng c·∫ßn ƒë·ªìng b·ªô h√≥a.
		‚úî D·ªÖ m·ªü r·ªông, ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi microservices, cloud-based.
		‚úî TƒÉng hi·ªáu su·∫•t, gi·∫£m t√†i nguy√™n b·ªô nh·ªõ.


	### üìå V√≠ d·ª• 2: Stateless Servlet x·ª≠ l√Ω t√≠nh to√°n nh∆∞ng kh√¥ng gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i 
	
			@WebServlet("/calculate")
			public class CalculationServlet extends HttpServlet {
				protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest req, HttpServletResponse resp) throws IOException {
					int a = Integer.parseInt(req.getParameter("a"));
					int b = Integer.parseInt(req.getParameter("b"));
					int sum = a + b;
					
					resp.getWriter().println("Sum: " + sum);
				}
			}

		üöÄ ƒêi·ªÉm m·∫°nh:

		D·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë∆∞·ª£c truy·ªÅn qua request, kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr√™n server.
		C√≥ th·ªÉ scale out d·ªÖ d√†ng b·∫±ng load balancer.



# Stateless Servlet trong Java EE 
	
Trong Java EE truy·ªÅn th·ªëng, b·∫°n c√≥ th·ªÉ t·∫°o m·ªôt Stateless Servlet b·∫±ng c√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng @WebServlet. V√≠ d·ª•:

	## ƒêi·ªÉm ch√≠nh c·ªßa Stateless Servlet 
		
			- Kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i gi·ªØa c√°c request.
			- M·ªói request ƒë∆∞·ª£c x·ª≠ l√Ω ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p, kh√¥ng c√≥ session ho·∫∑c d·ªØ li·ªáu c·ª•c b·ªô (instance variables).
			- C√≥ th·ªÉ m·ªü r·ªông d·ªÖ d√†ng m√† kh√¥ng lo v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ ƒë·ªìng b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªØa c√°c thread.





# Stateless Servlet trong Spring 
	Trong Spring, b·∫°n kh√¥ng c·∫ßn d√πng Servlet tr·ª±c ti·∫øp m√† thay th·∫ø b·∫±ng Spring Controller, v√¨ Spring Boot s·ª≠ d·ª•ng DispatcherServlet ƒë·ªÉ x·ª≠ l√Ω request.

	# üîπ Kh√°c bi·ªát gi·ªØa Stateless Servlet v√† Spring Controller 
	
	
	Feature				Stateless Servlet (Java EE)								Spring Controller
	Tri·ªÉn khai				K·∫ø th·ª´a HttpServlet										D√πng @RestController
	X·ª≠ l√Ω request			D√πng doGet(), doPost()									D√πng @GetMapping, @PostMapping
	C·∫•u h√¨nh				web.xml ho·∫∑c @WebServlet								Spring Boot t·ª± ƒë·ªông c·∫•u h√¨nh
	Qu·∫£n l√Ω lifecycle		Java EE container qu·∫£n l√Ω								Spring container qu·∫£n l√Ω

	
	
# 	Stateless vs Stateful trong Spring 
	
	
	## Stateless (Kh√¥ng c√≥ tr·∫°ng th√°i)
		
		- M·ªói request ƒë∆∞·ª£c x·ª≠ l√Ω ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p.
		
		- Kh√¥ng gi·ªØ d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªØa c√°c request (VD: kh√¥ng d√πng instance variables).
		
		- D·ªÖ d√†ng scale v√¨ kh√¥ng c√≥ tr·∫°ng th√°i c·∫ßn ƒë·ªìng b·ªô.
		
		
		
	## Stateful (C√≥ tr·∫°ng th√°i) 
		
		- Gi·ªØ d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªØa c√°c request b·∫±ng session ho·∫∑c shared state.
		
		- C·∫ßn c∆° ch·∫ø ƒë·ªìng b·ªô n·∫øu ch·∫°y tr√™n nhi·ªÅu instance.
	
	
	
	
	## V√≠ d·ª• v·ªÅ Stateful Bean (Kh√¥ng ph·∫£i Stateless!)

		@RequestMapping("/stateful")
		@SessionScope  // ‚ö†Ô∏è L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i tr√™n session (Stateful)

			@GetMapping
			public String statefulResponse() {
				counter++;
				return "Request count: " + counter;
			}
		}
		‚û° M·ªói request s·∫Ω tƒÉng gi√° tr·ªã counter, nghƒ©a l√† servlet n√†y c√≥ tr·∫°ng th√°i.
	
	
	
‚úî N·∫øu h·ªá th·ªëng c·∫ßn hi·ªáu nƒÉng cao, d·ªÖ scale, th√¨ n√™n d√πng stateless (@RestController).
‚úî N·∫øu c·∫ßn gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i gi·ªØa c√°c request (VD: shopping cart), th√¨ c√≥ th·ªÉ d√πng stateful, nh∆∞ng c·∫ßn c√¢n nh·∫Øc v·ªÅ ƒë·ªìng b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu.

üëâ T√≥m l·∫°i: Trong Spring, kh√¥ng c·∫ßn d√πng @WebServlet, thay v√†o ƒë√≥, d√πng @RestController v√† gi·ªØ ki·∫øn tr√∫c stateless cho h·ªá th·ªëng linh ho·∫°t h∆°n. üöÄ	




# 3. So s√°nh ThreadLocal v√† Stateless Servlet 


	üî• Ti√™u ch√≠							üèÜ ThreadLocal												üöÄ Stateless Servlet
	L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i		‚úÖ C√≥ (cho t·ª´ng thread)													‚ùå Kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i
	Thread safety		‚úÖ An to√†n (v√¨ m·ªói thread c√≥ m·ªôt b·∫£n sao ri√™ng)							‚úÖ An to√†n (v√¨ kh√¥ng l∆∞u bi·∫øn instance)
	·ª®ng d·ª•ng ch√≠nh		L∆∞u th√¥ng tin user session, transaction, DB connection					REST API, microservices, scalable system
	Hi·ªáu su·∫•t			‚ö° Cao (v√¨ kh√¥ng c·∫ßn synchronized) nh∆∞ng c√≥ nguy c∆° memory leak			‚ö° Cao (v√¨ kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i)
	Kh·∫£ nƒÉng m·ªü r·ªông	‚ùå Kh√¥ng t·ªët (ch·ªâ ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông trong ph·∫°m vi JVM)							‚úÖ T·ªët, d·ªÖ scale
	B·∫£o m·∫≠t				‚ùå N·∫øu kh√¥ng remove(), c√≥ th·ªÉ b·ªã r√≤ r·ªâ d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªØa c√°c request			‚úÖ B·∫£o m·∫≠t t·ªët, kh√¥ng l∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu d√†i h·∫°n



# Khi n√†o d√πng ThreadLocal & Stateless Servlet?
 


üöÄ T√¨nh hu·ªëng						‚úÖ N√™n d√πng ThreadLocal															‚úÖ N√™n d√πng Stateless Servlet
L∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu theo request		N·∫øu c·∫ßn gi·ªØ bi·∫øn trong c√πng m·ªôt thread (VD: User Session, Transaction).			N·∫øu ch·ªâ c·∫ßn x·ª≠ l√Ω request ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p, kh√¥ng gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i.
·ª®ng d·ª•ng REST API				‚ùå Kh√¥ng ph√π h·ª£p																‚úÖ C·ª±c k·ª≥ ph√π h·ª£p
·ª®ng d·ª•ng Microservices			‚ùå Kh√¥ng ph√π h·ª£p (ThreadLocal ch·ªâ ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông trong JVM)							‚úÖ R·∫•t ph√π h·ª£p

H·ªá th·ªëng scale l·ªõn				‚ùå Kh√¥ng m·ªü r·ªông t·ªët															‚úÖ R·∫•t d·ªÖ scale
	



# üî• K·∫øt lu·∫≠n 

- N·∫øu c·∫ßn l∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu trong t·ª´ng thread, h√£y d√πng ThreadLocal.
- N·∫øu mu·ªën h·ªá th·ªëng d·ªÖ scale, t·ªëi ∆∞u REST API ho·∫∑c microservices, h√£y d√πng Stateless Servlet.

# Kh√°i ni·ªám 
	Trong Spring, Stateful li√™n quan ƒë·∫øn vi·ªác l∆∞u tr·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i gi·ªØa c√°c request ho·∫∑c gi·ªØa c√°c session c·ªßa ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng. ƒêi·ªÅu n√†y tr√°i ng∆∞·ª£c v·ªõi Stateless, n∆°i m·ªói request ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p v√† kh√¥ng gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i.
	
# 	Khi n√†o Stateful quan tr·ªçng trong h·ªá th·ªëng? 

	‚úî ·ª®ng d·ª•ng c·∫ßn l∆∞u tr·ªØ th√¥ng tin ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng (session, shopping cart, authentication, v.v.)

	‚úî ·ª®ng d·ª•ng c·∫ßn gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i tr√™n nhi·ªÅu b∆∞·ªõc (multi-step forms, wizard, v.v.)
	‚úî Khi c·∫ßn qu·∫£n l√Ω phi√™n l√†m vi·ªác (WebSocket, chat application, game servers, v.v.)


# C√°ch tri·ªÉn khai Stateful trong Spring
	Spring h·ªó tr·ª£ nhi·ªÅu c√°ch ƒë·ªÉ l∆∞u tr·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i, t√πy v√†o y√™u c·∫ßu c·ªßa h·ªá th·ªëng:

	## üîπ a) L∆∞u tr·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i trong Session (@SessionAttributes, HttpSession) 
			C√°ch n√†y gi√∫p gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i trong session c·ªßa ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng.
			S·ª≠ d·ª•ng @SessionAttributes ƒë·ªÉ l∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªØa c√°c request c·ªßa m·ªôt user.

									@RequestParam String item) {

		}


			üí° Gi·∫£i th√≠ch:
			
			@SessionAttributes("cart") l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i c·ªßa cart trong session c·ªßa user.
			Khi user th√™m s·∫£n ph·∫©m, gi·ªè h√†ng s·∫Ω gi·ªØ nguy√™n tr·∫°ng th√°i cho ƒë·∫øn khi session b·ªã h·ªßy.
			‚û° Nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm: Kh√¥ng ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi h·ªá th·ªëng c√≥ nhi·ªÅu server (horizontal scaling) v√¨ session l∆∞u tr√™n t·ª´ng server ri√™ng l·∫ª.






	## üîπ b) L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i v·ªõi HttpSession (Th·ªß c√¥ng h∆°n, nh∆∞ng linh ho·∫°t h∆°n)

					Ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c h·ªá th·ªëng c·∫ßn l∆∞u d·ªØ li·ªáu t·∫°m th·ªùi cho user ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p.




	## üîπ c) L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i b·∫±ng Stateful Bean (@Scope("session") ho·∫∑c @Scope("prototype"))
	Spring h·ªó tr·ª£ Bean c√≥ tr·∫°ng th√°i th√¥ng qua scope:
	

		Scope						M√¥ t·∫£
		singleton				Ch·ªâ c√≥ m·ªôt instance duy nh·∫•t trong to√†n b·ªô ·ª©ng d·ª•ng (Stateless).
		prototype				M·ªói request t·∫°o m·ªôt instance m·ªõi (Stateful).
		session					M·ªôt instance duy tr√¨ trong su·ªët phi√™n l√†m vi·ªác c·ªßa user (Stateful).
		request					M·ªôt instance t·ªìn t·∫°i trong m·ªôt HTTP request (Stateless).



		### V√≠ d·ª•: L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i trong session b·∫±ng @SessionScope

		@SessionScope
		public class UserSession {

			}
		}
		

		### Controller s·ª≠ d·ª•ng Stateful Bean
		
		@Controller
		public class UserController {

			}
		}
				

			@Controller
			public class UserController {

					userSession.setUsername(name);

				@GetMapping("/getUser")
				@ResponseBody
				public String getUser() {
					return "User: " + userSession.getUsername();
				}
			}




	##  üîπ d) L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i v·ªõi Redis (H·ªó tr·ª£ Scaling t·ªët h∆°n) 
		Khi ch·∫°y h·ªá th·ªëng tr√™n nhi·ªÅu server (distributed system), s·ª≠ d·ª•ng session s·∫Ω g√¢y l·ªói v√¨ m·ªói server c√≥ session ri√™ng. ƒê·ªÉ gi·∫£i quy·∫øt, ta d√πng Redis ƒë·ªÉ l∆∞u session.

		üí° Gi·∫£i th√≠ch:
		D·ªØ li·ªáu session ƒë∆∞·ª£c l∆∞u v√†o Redis, gi√∫p c√≥ th·ªÉ scale ngang h·ªá th·ªëng m√† v·∫´n gi·ªØ session.



# 3. So s√°nh Stateful v√† Stateless trong Spring
	


Ti√™u ch√≠							Stateful														Stateless
L∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i			C√≥ gi·ªØ d·ªØ li·ªáu gi·ªØa c√°c request/session.						Kh√¥ng gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i gi·ªØa c√°c request.
Hi·ªáu su·∫•t				Ch·∫≠m h∆°n do ph·∫£i qu·∫£n l√Ω session/memory.						Nhanh h∆°n v√¨ kh√¥ng l∆∞u tr·∫°ng th√°i.
Kh·∫£ nƒÉng m·ªü r·ªông		H·∫°n ch·∫ø (c·∫ßn Redis, DB ƒë·ªÉ scale t·ªët).							D·ªÖ scale ngang (microservices).
·ª®ng d·ª•ng				Web app c√≥ ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p, gi·ªè h√†ng, multi-step forms.				REST API, Microservices, serverless.


# 4. Khi n√†o n√™n d√πng Stateful trong Spring?

		‚úî H·ªá th·ªëng Authentication (OAuth2, Session-based Auth)
		‚úî ·ª®ng d·ª•ng c√≥ gi·ªè h√†ng (Shopping Cart, Checkout Process)
		‚úî H·ªá th·ªëng chat real-time, WebSocket
		‚úî ·ª®ng d·ª•ng c·∫ßn l∆∞u th√¥ng tin t·∫°m th·ªùi cho t·ª´ng user (multi-step forms, wizards)
		‚úî H·ªá th·ªëng ng√¢n h√†ng, giao d·ªãch t√†i ch√≠nh (c·∫ßn gi·ªØ tr·∫°ng th√°i giao d·ªãch t·∫°m th·ªùi)
		
		üöÄ T√≥m l·∫°i:
		
		Stateful ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c h·ªá th·ªëng c·∫ßn l∆∞u tr·ªØ d·ªØ li·ªáu c·ªßa ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng trong su·ªët phi√™n l√†m vi·ªác.
		Stateless ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi microservices, REST API, gi√∫p h·ªá th·ªëng d·ªÖ m·ªü r·ªông h∆°n.
		Redis l√† m·ªôt gi·∫£i ph√°p t·ªët n·∫øu c·∫ßn Stateful nh∆∞ng v·∫´n mu·ªën h·ªá th·ªëng c√≥ th·ªÉ scale ngang.
		üí° L·ªùi khuy√™n: Khi thi·∫øt k·∫ø h·ªá th·ªëng, ∆∞u ti√™n Stateless, ch·ªâ d√πng Stateful khi th·ª±c s·ª± c·∫ßn thi·∫øt.

# java.base ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông th·∫ø n√†o ?

	üîπ b) java.base kh√¥ng ph·ª• thu·ªôc v√†o module n√†o kh√°c

		- Nh∆∞ng java.base kh√¥ng ph·ª• thu·ªôc v√†o b·∫•t k·ª≥ nh√≥m module n√†o kh√°c

# T·∫°i sao  java.base quan tr·ªçng trong h·ªá th·ªëng l·ªõn
